Black Iron Inc. 

NI 43-101 Technical Report – PEA of the Shymanivske Iron Ore Project 

 

 
 

 3-4 December 2011 
 
 
 

The following Qualified Persons (QP), as such term is defined by NI 43-101, have contributed to 

the writing of this Report and have provided the requisite QP certificates included at the 

beginning of this Report. The information contained in the certificates is outlined in the sections 

of this Report that each of the QPs are responsible for. 

 

 André Allaire,  BBA 

 Hugues de Corta,  Independent 

 Richard Risto,  WGM 

 

The individuals listed below, who have contributed to the completion of the PEA Study and to 

this Report, have extensive experience in the mining and metals industry or in a supporting 

capacity in the industry. They are not considered as QPs as defined by NI 43-101, for the 

purpose of this Report. 

 

 Nikola Vukovic  M.Eng. (Mining Engineering)  BBA 

 Enzo Palumbo  M.Eng. (Metallurgical Engineering) BBA 

 Angelo Grandillo  M. Eng. (Metallurgical Engineering) BBA 

 Farshid Ghazanfari  Geologist    Black Iron 

     Iron Ore Market Specialists  CRU Strategies 

 

Black Iron retained the services of CRU Strategies, a division of CRU Limited, to perform a 

market study to evaluate potential target markets for the Black Iron Shymanivske iron ore 

concentrate and/or pellets. BBA has reviewed the contents of the market study report and 

believes that it provides a reasonable overview of the past and current iron ore market as well 

as projections according to various recognized sources. 

 

Drill core samples collected and prepared by Black Iron were submitted to Mekhanobrchermet 

Institute in Kryviy Rih in Ukraine, and SGS Lakefield Research in Lakefield Ontario, which is an 

accredited laboratory. Although BBA has reviewed the testwork results generated by 

Mekhanobrchermet and SGS and believes that they are generally accurate, BBA is relying on 

Mekhanobrchermet and SGS as independent experts.

Section 7a- MagFe Blocks and Pit Outline



 
 

Black Iron Inc. 

NI 43-101 Technical Report – PEA of the Shymanivske Iron Ore Project 

 

 
 
 

  December 2011 

 
 
 

 

 

 

 

 

 

 

Appendix C 

 

Risk Register 



N° Risk Title Risk Description Category
Consequence 
(Description)

Probability Manageability Mitigation Comment

1.1.1.1 Select credible/reputable consultant for 
assisting with the environmental permits

Clarification on difference between 
domestic and international standards

1.1.1.2 Make assumptions for major project 
parameters (final pit depth, pellet plant etc..)
1.1.1.3 Create environmental road map
1.1.1.4 Create a dedicated team dealing with all 
the environmental issues
1.1.1.5 Accelerate baseline monitoring program
1.1.1.6 Begin discussion with Ukrainian authorities 
and start land acquisition

2.1.1.1 Confirm project land requirements Be aware of politics and system delays 

2.1.1.2 Develop road map for land acquisition
2.1.1.3 Select reputable and experienced service 
provider

3.1.1. Delayed plant start up Low Medium
3.1.1.1 Start early negotiation with Government 
and Private suppliers
3.1.1.2 Establish power requirements and 
benchmark against existing projects
3.1.1.3 Establish grid accessibility 

CAPEX 4.1.1. Increased CAPEX to build rail spur Low Medium 4.1.1.1 Establish project rail requirements
Questionable availability/quality of local 
equipment
